					## List of all Logic Apps connectors
					
		
			 
				
					
		
			
				
			
			Feedback
		
	
				
		  
		
	 
		
			
				
					
				
				
					
						Summarize this article for me
					
				
			
			
			
		
	 
		
	
					
This page is a filtered version of the [Connector reference overview](./) page. Only **connectors available in Logic Apps** are shown.

You can select a connector to view more detailed connector-specific documentation including its functionality and region availability. You can also filter all connectors by a certain category. Note that filters do not stack and each link will take you to another page within the documentation site.

Please see details about all [Logic Apps regions](https://azure.microsoft.com/global-infrastructure/services/?products=logic-apps&regions=all).
All connectors are available in global regions.
Availability in special regions is shown in the table below.

### List of Connectors

	
		
		Connector name
		Us Gov
		DoD
		China cloud
